## Complete Architecture, Tech Stack & Implementation Blueprint

---

## 1. 🏗️ TECH STACK (Performance-First)

### **Frontend**
| Layer | Technology | Why |
|-------|-----------|-----|
| **Framework** | **Next.js 14+ (App Router)** | SSR/SSG, API routes, file-based routing, Vercel optimized |
| **Language** | TypeScript | Type safety across full stack |
| **Styling** | Tailwind CSS + shadcn/ui | Rapid, consistent, accessible component library |
| **State** | Zustand (global) + TanStack Query (server) | Lightweight, performant data fetching |
| **Animations** | Framer Motion | Smooth transitions, page loads, micro-interactions |
| **Charts** | Recharts / Tremor | Analytics dashboards |
| **Tables** | TanStack Table v8 | Handle 10k+ rows with virtualization |
| **Forms** | React Hook Form + Zod | Validation, performance |
| **PDF/Excel** | jsPDF + SheetJS | Export functionality |

### **Backend**
| Layer | Technology | Why |
|-------|-----------|-----|
| **Runtime** | Node.js / Bun | Bun for 3x faster builds & runtime |
| **Framework** | Next.js API Routes + tRPC or REST | Type-safe APIs |
| **Auth** | NextAuth.js v5 (Auth.js) + JWT | Role-based access, session management |
| **Validation** | Zod | Shared schemas frontend ↔ backend |

### **Database**
| Layer | Technology | Why |
|-------|-----------|-----|
| **Primary DB** | **PostgreSQL** | Relational data, complex queries, ACID |
| **ORM** | Prisma | Type-safe queries, migrations, relations |
| **Cache** | Redis (Upstash) | Sessions, OTPs, frequently accessed data |
| **Search** | PostgreSQL Full-Text / Algolia (later) | Fast member search |

### **Storage & Infrastructure**
| Service | Use |
|---------|-----|
| **AWS S3 / Cloudflare R2** | Member photos, documents, gym gallery |
| **Vercel / AWS EC2** | Hosting |
| **CDN** | Cloudflare / Vercel Edge | Global static asset delivery |

## 3. 👥 ROLE-BASED ACCESS CONTROL (RBAC)

### **Hierarchy**
```
SUPER ADMIN (God Mode)
    └── Can create Admins
    └── Can override ANY restriction
    └── Can see audit logs of ALL admins
    └── Can assign/remove panel access
    └── Can configure global settings
    └── Can manage subscription PLANS
    └── Can export EVERYTHING

ADMIN (Manager)
    ├── Can manage members, trainers, staff
    ├── Can view financial reports (restricted: can't see super admin pricing/costs)
    ├── Can assign trainers to members
    ├── Can manage subscriptions (can't delete plans, only pause/activate)
    ├── Can import/export data (batch limit: 5k rows vs Super Admin unlimited)
    ├── Can view analytics (restricted: can't see profit margins if super admin hides)
    └── Cannot: Delete other admins, change global config, see audit logs

RECEPTIONIST
    ├── Member check-in/check-out
    ├── Register walk-in members
    ├── View member profiles (read-only)
    ├── Collect payments (cash/card entry)
    ├── Print/view receipts
    └── Cannot: See financial reports, delete data

TRAINER
    ├── View assigned members
    ├── Create workout plans & diet charts
    ├── Track member progress (weight, measurements)
    ├── Schedule PT sessions
    ├── Mark attendance for sessions
    └── Cannot: See payments, other trainers' clients (unless assigned)

MEMBER (Customer Panel)
    ├── View own profile & subscription status
    ├── View workout plan assigned by trainer
    ├── Track personal progress (charts)
    ├── Book/schedule PT sessions
    ├── View payment history & download receipts
    ├── Raise complaints/requests
    └── Update personal details

WORKER/STAFF
    ├── Mark equipment maintenance
    ├── View cleaning/maintenance schedule
    ├── Report issues
    └── Limited read access
```

### **Permission Matrix (Example)**
| Feature | Super Admin | Admin | Receptionist | Trainer | Member |
|---------|:-----------:|:-----:|:------------:|:-------:|:------:|
| Create Member | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ |
| Delete Member | ✅ | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |
| Edit Subscription Plan | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |
| View All Finances | ✅ | ⚠️ Partial | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |
| Export Data | ✅ Unlimited | ✅ 5k rows | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |
| Assign Roles | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |
| Audit Logs | ✅ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ | ❌ |

## 4. 🗄️ DATABASE SCHEMA (Prisma)

```prisma
// Core Users
model User {
  id            String    @id @default(cuid())
  email         String    @unique
  phone         String?   @unique
  password      String    // hashed
  firstName     String
  lastName      String
  avatar        String?
  role          Role      @default(MEMBER)
  status        Status    @default(ACTIVE)
  createdAt     DateTime  @default(now())
  updatedAt     DateTime  @updatedAt
  
  // Relations
  member        Member?
  trainer       Trainer?
  receptionist  Receptionist?
  admin         Admin?
  superAdmin    SuperAdmin?
  sessions      Session[]
  notifications Notification[]
  auditLogs     AuditLog[]
}

enum Role {
  SUPER_ADMIN
  ADMIN
  RECEPTIONIST
  TRAINER
  MEMBER
  WORKER
}

// Member Profile
model Member {
  id              String   @id @default(cuid())
  userId          String   @unique
  user            User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id])
  
  // Physical
  dateOfBirth     DateTime?
  gender          Gender?
  bloodGroup      String?
  emergencyContact String?
  address         String?
  
  // Gym Specific
  joinDate        DateTime @default(now())
  membershipType  String   // Monthly, Quarterly, Yearly
  subscription    Subscription?
  attendance      Attendance[]
  progress        Progress[]
  workouts        WorkoutPlan[]
  payments        Payment[]
  trainerId       String?
  trainer         Trainer? @relation(fields: [trainerId], references: [id])
}

// Subscription Management
model Subscription {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  memberId    String   @unique
  member      Member   @relation(fields: [memberId], references: [id])
  
  planId      String
  plan        Plan     @relation(fields: [planId], references: [id])
  
  startDate   DateTime
  endDate     DateTime
  amount      Decimal
  status      SubStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  autoRenew   Boolean  @default(false)
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
}

model Plan {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  name        String   // "Gold", "Silver", "Platinum"
  duration    Int      // days
  price       Decimal
  features    Json     // ["Cardio", "Weights", "Steam", "PT 4 sessions"]
  isActive    Boolean  @default(true)
  createdBy   String   // super admin only
  subscriptions Subscription[]
}

// Trainer Profile
model Trainer {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  userId      String   @unique
  user        User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id])
  specialization String[]
  experience  Int      // years
  salary      Decimal?
  members     Member[]
  schedules   Schedule[]
}

// Attendance (QR/Biometric/Face)
model Attendance {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  memberId    String
  member      Member   @relation(fields: [memberId], references: [id])
  date        DateTime @default(now())
  checkIn     DateTime
  checkOut    DateTime?
  status      AttStatus @default(PRESENT)
}

// Payments
model Payment {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  memberId    String
  member      Member   @relation(fields: [memberId], references: [id])
  amount      Decimal
  method      PayMethod // CASH, CARD, UPI, ONLINE
  type        PayType   // SUBSCRIPTION, PT_SESSION, PRODUCT
  status      PayStatus @default(PENDING)
  receiptNo   String   @unique
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
}

// Equipment & Maintenance
model Equipment {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  name        String
  category    String   // Cardio, Strength, Free Weights
  purchaseDate DateTime
  warranty    DateTime?
  status      EqStatus @default(WORKING)
  lastService DateTime?
  nextService DateTime?
  logs        MaintLog[]
}

model MaintLog {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  equipmentId String
  equipment   Equipment @relation(fields: [equipmentId], references: [id])
  issue       String
  resolvedBy  String?
  cost        Decimal?
  status      String
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
}

// Audit Logs (Super Admin Only)
model AuditLog {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  userId      String
  user        User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id])
  action      String   // "CREATED_MEMBER", "DELETED_PLAN"
  entityType  String   // "Member", "Payment"
  entityId    String?
  oldValue    Json?
  newValue    Json?
  ipAddress   String?
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
}

// Notifications
model Notification {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  userId      String
  user        User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id])
  title       String
  message     String
  type        NotifType
  isRead      Boolean  @default(false)
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
}
```

## 5. 📊 DATA FLOW ARCHITECTURE

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                        CLIENT SIDE                           │
│  ┌─────────┐ ┌─────────┐ ┌─────────┐ ┌─────────┐          │
│  │ Member  │ │ Admin   │ │Trainer  │ │Reception│          │
│  │  Panel  │ │  Panel  │ │ Panel   │ │  Panel  │          │
│  └────┬────┘ └────┬────┘ └────┬────┘ └────┬────┘          │
│       │           │           │           │                │
│       └───────────┴─────┬─────┴───────────┘                │
│                         ▼                                   │
│              ┌─────────────────────┐                        │
│              │   Next.js App Router │                        │
│              │  (Middleware + RBAC) │                        │
│              └──────────┬──────────┘                        │
└─────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────┘
                          │
                          ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      API LAYER (tRPC/REST)                   │
│  ┌─────────────┐ ┌─────────────┐ ┌─────────────────────┐   │
│  │ Auth Router │ │Member Router│ │Analytics Router     │   │
│  │  (Auth.js)  │ │  (CRUD)     │ │ (Aggregations)      │   │
│  └─────────────┘ └─────────────┘ └─────────────────────┘   │
│  ┌─────────────┐ ┌─────────────┐ ┌─────────────────────┐   │
│  │Payment Router│ │Import/Export │ │Notification Router  │   │
│  │  (Razorpay) │ │ (Streaming)  │ │ (WebSockets/SSE)    │   │
│  └─────────────┘ └─────────────┘ └─────────────────────┘   │
└─────────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┘
                          │
              ┌───────────┼───────────┐
              ▼           ▼           ▼
        ┌─────────┐ ┌─────────┐ ┌─────────┐
        │PostgreSQL│ │  Redis  │ │   S3    │
        │ (Prisma) │ (Cache)  │ (Files)  │
        └─────────┘ └─────────┘ └─────────┘
```

## 6. 🚀 KEY FEATURES & MODULES

### **A. Super Admin Command Center**
- **Global Dashboard**: Real-time member count, revenue, active subscriptions, attendance heatmap
- **Admin Management**: Create/edit admins, toggle their permissions (the 2-5% restrictions)
- **Audit Trail**: Every action by every user logged with IP, timestamp, before/after values
- **System Config**: Gym name, logo, working hours, notification templates, backup settings
- **Revenue Analytics**: Profit/loss, subscription trends, trainer performance, peak hours

### **B. Admin Panel**
- **Member Management**: Bulk import (CSV/Excel), bulk export, advanced filters
- **Staff Management**: Trainers schedule, receptionist shifts, worker assignments
- **Financial Reports**: Daily collection, pending payments, expense tracking
- **Subscription Control**: Activate/pause/renew, but cannot delete plans created by super admin
- **Attendance Overview**: Who's in the gym right now (live view)

### **C. Receptionist Desk**
- **Quick Check-in**: Search member → Mark present → Print token
- **Walk-in Registration**: Quick form with photo capture (webcam)
- **Payment Collection**: Record cash/UPI/card, auto-generate receipt PDF
- **Today's Schedule**: View all PT sessions for the day

### **D. Trainer Dashboard**
- **My Members**: List with progress indicators
- **Workout Builder**: Drag-drop exercise builder with sets/reps/rest
- **Diet Planner**: Pre-built templates + custom plans
- **Progress Tracking**: Weight, body fat, measurements over time (charts)
- **Session Calendar**: Book/manage PT slots

### **E. Member Portal**
- **Digital Membership Card**: With QR code for check-in
- **My Progress**: Visual charts of body metrics
- **Workout Plan**: Today's exercises with video demos
- **Book Trainer**: View available slots & book PT
- **Payments**: History + download invoices
- **Refer & Earn**: Referral code system

### **F. Import/Export Engine** 📁
**Import:**
- Streaming CSV/Excel parser (Papa Parse / SheetJS)
- Chunk processing (100 rows at a time) — no UI freeze
- Validation pipeline: Check duplicates, invalid phone, missing fields
- Progress bar with error log (download failed rows)
- Template download for bulk upload

**Export:**
- Server-side generation for large datasets (10k+)
- Formats: CSV, Excel (.xlsx), PDF (professional branded reports)
- Filtered exports (date range, status, plan type)
- Background job + email delivery for huge exports

---

## 7. ⚡ PERFORMANCE OPTIMIZATIONS

| Strategy | Implementation |
|----------|---------------|
| **Database** | Connection pooling (PgBouncer), indexed queries, read replicas |
| **Frontend** | Next.js streaming, React Suspense, lazy load panels, image optimization |
| **Tables** | TanStack Table virtualization → smooth 50k rows |
| **API** | tRPC batching, request deduplication, pagination (cursor-based) |
| **Cache** | Redis for sessions, SWR for client cache, CDN for static assets |
| **Import** | Web Workers for CSV parsing, chunked DB inserts |
| **Export** | Stream response, don't load all into memory |
| **Images** | Next.js Image component, WebP format, lazy loading |
| **Bundle** | Code splitting by role, tree shaking |

## 11. 💡 CUSTOM LOADER IMPLEMENTATION IDEA

```tsx
// components/loaders/DumbbellLoader.tsx
"use client";
import { motion } from "framer-motion";

export const DumbbellLoader = () => (
  <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-4">
    <div className="relative w-24 h-8">
      {/* Bar */}
      <div className="absolute top-1/2 left-0 right-0 h-1 bg-gold rounded-full" />
      {/* Left Weight */}
      <motion.div
        className="absolute left-0 top-0 w-6 h-8 bg-gradient-to-b from-gold to-amber-600 rounded-lg"
        animate={{ rotate: 360 }}
        transition={{ duration: 1.5, repeat: Infinity, ease: "linear" }}
        style={{ originX: 0.5, originY: 0.5 }}
      />
      {/* Right Weight */}
      <motion.div
        className="absolute right-0 top-0 w-6 h-8 bg-gradient-to-b from-gold to-amber-600 rounded-lg"
        animate={{ rotate: -360 }}
        transition={{ duration: 1.5, repeat: Infinity, ease: "linear" }}
      />
    </div>
    <motion.p 
      className="text-gold font-bold tracking-widest text-sm"
      animate={{ opacity: [0.5, 1, 0.5] }}
      transition={{ duration: 2, repeat: Infinity }}
    >
      EAGLE GYM
    </motion.p>
  </div>
);
```

## Complete Feature Expansion + Revolutionary UI/UX Overhaul

---

## 🎨 PART 1: REVOLUTIONARY UI/UX SYSTEM

### **Design Philosophy: "Liquid Gold & Obsidian"**

Forget basic dark mode. This is a **cinematic, immersive experience** that makes users feel like they're using a premium fitness app, not a boring admin panel.

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  THEME TOKENS                                               │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Background Primary:   #050505 (True Obsidian)              │
│  Background Elevated:  #0A0A0A (Glass base)                 │
│  Background Card:      rgba(15, 15, 15, 0.8) + backdrop blur│
│  Primary Gold:         #FFD700 (Liquid Gold)                │
│  Gold Gradient:        linear-gradient(135deg, #FFD700, #FFA500, #FF8C00) │
│  Accent Electric:      #00F0FF (Cyan pulse)                 │
│  Success Neon:         #39FF14 (Neon Green)                 │
│  Danger Glow:          #FF3131 (Crimson)                    │
│  Text Primary:         #FFFFFF                              │
│  Text Secondary:       rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.6)             │
│  Text Muted:           rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.35)            │
│  Border Subtle:        rgba(255, 215, 0, 0.15)              │
│  Border Glow:          rgba(255, 215, 0, 0.4)               │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

---

### **Visual Effects & Atmosphere**

| Element | Specification |
|---------|--------------|
| **Glassmorphism Cards** | `background: rgba(15,15,15,0.7)`, `backdrop-filter: blur(20px)`, `border: 1px solid rgba(255,215,0,0.1)`, subtle inner shadow |
| **Gold Border Glow** | On hover: `box-shadow: 0 0 20px rgba(255,215,0,0.15), inset 0 0 20px rgba(255,215,0,0.05)` |
| **Ambient Background** | Very subtle animated mesh gradient (dark purple → deep black → dark gold) moving slowly behind content |
| **Noise Texture** | 2% opacity grain overlay on all backgrounds for tactile feel |
| **Spotlight Cursor** | Radial gradient follows mouse on dashboard cards (subtle gold highlight) |
| **Scroll Behavior** | Smooth scroll with momentum, parallax on hero sections |
| **Page Transitions** | Framer Motion: Fade + slight Y-translate (20px → 0), 0.4s, ease-out-expo |

---

### **Typography System**

```
Display:    "Clash Display" or "Bebas Neue" — 72px, tracking tight, ALL CAPS for headers
Headings:   "Inter" — Bold, tight line height (1.1)
Body:       "Inter" or "Satoshi" — Regular/Medium, 16px, line height 1.6
Numbers:    "JetBrains Mono" or "SF Mono" — For stats, prices, counters
Accent:     "Cinzel" or "Playfair Display" — For elegant quotes, member names
```

**Type Scale:**
- **Hero**: 64px / 4rem (Mobile: 36px)
- **H1**: 48px / 3rem (Mobile: 28px)
- **H2**: 36px / 2.25rem (Mobile: 24px)
- **H3**: 24px / 1.5rem (Mobile: 20px)
- **Body Large**: 18px
- **Body**: 16px
- **Caption**: 12px / uppercase / tracking-widest / gold color

---

### **Custom Loader: "The Golden Eagle"**

```
PHASE 1: Black screen
PHASE 2: Golden particle dust swirls from center
PHASE 3: Particles form an abstract eagle silhouette
PHASE 4: Eagle grabs a dumbbell (rotates 360°)
PHASE 5: "EAGLE GYM" types out with gold shimmer
PHASE 6: Fades to dashboard
```

**Implementation**: Lottie JSON + CSS particles. Duration: 2.5s max.

### **Component Design Specifications**

#### **Stat Cards**
```
┌─────────────────────────────┐
│  👤                         │
│  Total Members              │
│  ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━    │
│  1,247          ↑ 12%       │
│  ─────────────────────────  │
│  [Sparkline chart]          │
└─────────────────────────────┘

Style:
- Background: Glassmorphism
- Border: 1px solid rgba(255,215,0,0.08)
- Border-radius: 24px
- Padding: 24px
- Hover: Border glows gold, card lifts 4px (transform: translateY)
- Number: JetBrains Mono, 36px, Gold gradient text
- Icon: 40px container, gold background at 10% opacity, rounded-2xl
```

#### **Data Tables**
```
┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  Members                    [Filter ▼] [Export ⬇] │
├────┬─────────────┬──────────┬──────────┬─────────┤
│ □  │ NAME        │ PLAN     │ STATUS   │ ACTIONS │
├────┼─────────────┼──────────┼──────────┼─────────┤
│ □  │ ◉ Rahul P.  │ 💎 Gold  │ 🟢 Active│ ⋮       │
│    │ +91 98xxx   │ 45 days  │          │         │
├────┼─────────────┼──────────┼──────────┼─────────┤
│ □  │ ◉ Priya S.  │ 🥈 Silver│ 🟡 Due   │ ⋮       │
└────┴─────────────┴──────────┴──────────┴─────────┘

Features:
- Sticky header with blur backdrop
- Row hover: subtle gold left border appears + row highlight
- Checkbox: custom gold checkbox
- Avatar: 40px circle with status dot (green/yellow/red pulse)
- Actions: 3-dot menu with slide-out options
- Pagination: Infinite scroll OR numbered with gold active state
- Empty state: Illustrated eagle with "No members found" in elegant font
```

#### **Buttons**
```
Primary:   Gold gradient background, black text, rounded-full, hover: brightness up + shadow
Secondary: Transparent, gold border, gold text, hover: gold background fills from left
Danger:    Crimson glow, hover: intensify
Ghost:     No border, text only, hover: subtle background
Fab:       Floating action, gold circle, shadow-lg, pulse animation on attention
```

#### **Inputs**
```
- Background: rgba(255,255,255,0.03)
- Border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1)
- Border-radius: 16px
- Focus: Border turns gold + subtle glow
- Label: Floats up on focus (floating label pattern)
- Icon left: Gold at 50% opacity
- Error: Crimson border + shake animation
```

#### **Modals/Drawers**
```
- Backdrop: rgba(0,0,0,0.8) + backdrop blur
- Panel: Glassmorphism, border-radius 24px (top on mobile)
- Entry: Slide up from bottom (mobile) / Scale in (desktop)
- Exit: Reverse
- Close: Top right, gold X, hover: rotate 90deg
```

#### **Notifications (Toast)**
```
- Slide in from right (desktop) / bottom (mobile)
- Glass background
- Left accent bar (color by type)
- Auto-dismiss with progress bar at bottom
- Action buttons inline
```

---

### **Responsive Breakpoints**

| Name | Width | Behavior |
|------|-------|----------|
| **Mobile** | < 640px | Bottom nav, stacked cards, full-width drawers, hamburger menu |
| **Tablet** | 640-1024px | Collapsible sidebar (icons only), 2-column grids |
| **Desktop** | 1024-1440px | Full sidebar, 3-4 column grids, side panels |
| **Ultrawide** | > 1440px | Max-width container centered, more whitespace, bigger charts |

---

### **Animation Specifications**

| Interaction | Animation |
|-------------|-----------|
| **Page Load** | Stagger fade-in (0.05s delay per element) |
| **Card Hover** | `translateY(-4px)`, border glow, 0.3s ease |
| **Button Press** | Scale to 0.97, 0.1s |
| **Tab Switch** | Underline slides to active tab (spring physics) |
| **Chart Load** | Bars grow from bottom, line draws itself, 1s |
| **Number Counter** | Count up from 0, 1.5s, easeOutExpo |
| **Table Row Appear** | Fade + slide right, staggered |
| **Image Load** | Blur-up placeholder → sharp image |
| **Skeleton** | Shimmer animation (gold gradient sweep) |
| **Success Action** | Confetti burst (subtle, gold particles) |
| **Error Action** | Shake horizontal + red glow pulse |
| **New Notification** | Bell shake + badge bounce |
| **Check-in Success** | Green pulse ring expands from center |
| **Data Refresh** | Pull-to-refresh (mobile) / Spin button (desktop) |

## 🚀 PART 2: MASSIVE FEATURE EXPANSION

### **A. Smart Reception & Operations**

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **🖥️ Kiosk Mode** | Turn any tablet into a self-check-in station. Members scan QR → Auto check-in → Welcome message with name. No receptionist needed for regulars. |
| **📱 QR Digital Card** | Every member gets a beautiful digital membership card (Apple Wallet / Google Pay compatible) with QR code, photo, plan details. |
| **🎯 Visitor/Guest Pass** | Generate trial passes with expiry. Track walk-ins. Convert trials to members with one click. |
| **👥 Family/Corporate Plans** | Link multiple members under one payer. Corporate dashboards for HR to track employee usage. |
| **🔄 Membership Freeze** | Members can freeze membership (vacation/medical) with auto-resume date. Admin approval workflow. |
| **⬆️⬇️ Upgrade/Downgrade** | One-click plan changes with pro-rata billing calculation. |
| **🎁 Festival Offers** | Auto-apply Diwali, New Year offers. Countdown timers on member portal. |
| **💳 EMI Integration** | Integrate with Razorpay/Stripe for monthly EMI on annual plans. |

---

### **B. Group Classes & Scheduling**

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **🧘 Class Catalog** | Yoga, Zumba, CrossFit, Pilates, Spinning — each with description, trainer, intensity level, calories burn estimate. |
| **📅 Class Booking** | Members book slots. Waitlist auto-fills cancellations. Capacity limits with visual seat map. |
| **🎫 Class Passes** | Separate from membership — buy 5/10 class packs. |
| **📍 Studio/Room Booking** | Book specific rooms for PT sessions or group activities. |
| **⏰ Recurring Bookings** | "Every Monday-Wednesday-Friday at 6 AM" auto-book. |
| **🚫 No-Show Penalty** | Track no-shows. Auto-deduct from class pack or warn after 3 strikes. |
| **📊 Class Popularity** | Which classes are trending? Peak booking times? Auto-suggest new time slots. |

---

### **C. Body Transformation & Progress**

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **📸 Progress Photo Tracker** | Upload front/side/back photos monthly. **Before/After slider comparison** with date stamps. Privacy controls (member-only or shareable). |
| **📏 Measurements Log** | Chest, waist, hips, biceps, thighs, body fat %, weight. Visual line charts with goal lines. |
| **🎯 Goal Setting** | "Lose 10kg in 3 months" → Auto-creates milestone checkpoints. Celebrates when achieved (confetti + badge). |
| **🏆 Transformation Stories** | Admin can publish success stories (with permission) to motivate others. Beautiful gallery layout. |
| **📋 Fitness Assessment** | Initial assessment form: BMI, BMR, flexibility test, strength test, cardio test. Retest every month. |

---

### **D. Trainer Ecosystem**

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **💪 Trainer Marketplace** | Members browse trainer profiles (specialization, experience, rating, availability, price). Book trial sessions. |
| **⭐ Rating & Review** | Members rate trainers after sessions. 5-star system with comment. Trainers see aggregated feedback. |
| **📋 Session Notes** | Trainer writes private notes about each member's session. Member sees only workout plan. |
| **💰 Commission Auto-Calc** | Trainer gets % of PT session fees. Auto-calculated monthly. Payroll integration. |
| **📆 Availability Calendar** | Trainers block their unavailable hours. Members see real-time free slots. |
| **🎓 Certification Tracker** | Track trainer certifications with expiry alerts (ACE, NASM, etc.). |

---

### **E. Diet & Nutrition Module**

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **🍽️ Meal Logger** | Members log meals with photos. AI estimates calories (or manual entry). |
| **📊 Macro Tracker** | Protein, Carbs, Fats, Fiber, Water intake. Circular progress rings. |
| **🥗 Diet Plans** | Trainer assigns meal plans (Breakfast/Lunch/Dinner/Snacks). Recipe database with macros. |
| **💧 Water Reminder** | Push notification every 2 hours. Tap to log glass. Streak counter. |
| **🍎 Supplement Tracker** | Log protein, creatine, vitamins. Reminder notifications. |
| **📉 Calorie Calculator** | TDEE calculator based on activity level, goal (cut/bulk/maintain). |

---

### **F. Gamification Engine**

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **🎖️ Achievement Badges** | "First Week Warrior", "30-Day Streak", "Early Bird" (5 AM check-in), "Heavy Lifter" (personal record), "Social Butterfly" (referred 5 friends). |
| **🏅 Levels & XP** | Earn XP for: check-ins (10 XP), completing workouts (50 XP), hitting goals (100 XP), referring (200 XP). Level up from Bronze → Silver → Gold → Platinum → Diamond → Eagle Elite. |
| **🏆 Leaderboards** | "Most Check-ins This Month", "Highest Weight Lifted", "Most Consistent". Anonymous option for privacy. |
| **⚔️ Challenges** | Admin creates challenges: "30-Day Abs Challenge", "100kg Bench Press Club". Members join, track progress, see leaderboard. |
| **🎁 Reward Store** | XP converts to points → Redeem for: free protein shake, 1-day guest pass, merchandise discount, extra PT session. |

| Feature | Description |

### **H. Advanced Analytics & Intelligence**

| Feature | Description |
|---------|-------------|
| **🔥 Live Gym Occupancy** | Real-time count of members inside. Heatmap by hour/day. "Best time to gym" recommendation. |
| **💰 Revenue Intelligence** | MRR (Monthly Recurring Revenue), ARPU (Average Revenue Per User), Churn Rate, LTV (Lifetime Value). Predictive forecasting. |
| **⚠️ Churn Prediction** | ML-based: "Member hasn't come in 15 days + payment due = 85% churn risk". Auto-trigger win-back campaign. |
| **📈 Attendance Heatmap** | Calendar view colored by attendance density. Identify dead hours for promotions. |
| **🏋️ Equipment Usage** | Which machines are used most? Which are idle? Optimize floor layout. Predict maintenance. |
| **👥 Cohort Analysis** | "Members who joined in January — how many are still active?" Retention curves. |
| **🎯 Lead Funnel** | Walk-in → Trial → Member → Referrer. Conversion rates at each stage. |

## 🗄️ PART 4: UPDATED DATABASE (Key New Tables)

```prisma
// NEW: Gamification
model Achievement {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  name        String   // "Early Bird", "Iron Man"
  description String
  icon        String   // Lucide icon name or URL
  xpValue     Int
  condition   Json     // {type: "CHECKIN_STREAK", count: 30}
  users       UserAchievement[]
}

model UserAchievement {
  id            String      @id @default(cuid())
  userId        String
  achievementId String
  achievedAt    DateTime    @default(now())
}

model XPTransaction {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  userId      String
  amount      Int
  reason      String   // "Check-in", "Workout Complete"
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
}

// NEW: Group Classes
model GymClass {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  name        String   // "Power Yoga"
  description String
  trainerId   String
  maxCapacity Int
  duration    Int      // minutes
  color       String   // hex for calendar
  schedules   ClassSchedule[]
}

model ClassSchedule {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  classId     String
  dayOfWeek   Int      // 0-6
  startTime   String   // "18:00"
  room        String
  bookings    ClassBooking[]
}

model ClassBooking {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  scheduleId  String
  memberId    String
  status      BookingStatus @default(CONFIRMED)
  bookedAt    DateTime @default(now())
}

// NEW: Progress Photos
model ProgressPhoto {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  memberId    String
  photoUrl    String
  photoType   String   // FRONT, SIDE, BACK
  takenAt     DateTime @default(now())
  weight      Float?   // kg at time of photo
}

// NEW: Chat System
model Conversation {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  participants String[] // user IDs
  messages    Message[]
  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt
}

model Message {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  conversationId String
  senderId    String
  content     String
  attachments String[] // URLs
  readBy      String[]
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
}

// NEW: Inventory/POS
model Product {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  name        String
  category    String   // SUPPLEMENT, MERCHANDISE, BEVERAGE
  price       Decimal
  costPrice   Decimal
  stock       Int
  barcode     String?
  image       String?
}

model Sale {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  items       Json     // [{productId, qty, price}]
  total       Decimal
  paymentMethod String
  customerId  String?  // member or walk-in
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
}

// NEW: Notifications
model Notification {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  userId      String
  title       String
  body        String
  type        String   // PAYMENT_DUE, CLASS_REMINDER, ACHIEVEMENT
  data        Json?    // extra payload
  isRead      Boolean  @default(false)
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
}
```

## 🎯 PART 5: NEW IMPLEMENTATION ROADMAP

### **Phase 1: Foundation + Stunning UI (Week 1-2)**
- [ ] Next.js 14 setup with App Router
- [ ] Design system: All tokens, components, animations
- [ ] Custom Eagle + Dumbbell loader (Lottie)
- [ ] Auth system with role-based redirects
- [ ] Glassmorphism sidebar + responsive layout
- [ ] **Dark Obsidian + Liquid Gold theme applied globally**
- [ ] Command palette (Cmd+K) for instant navigation

### **Phase 2: Core + Reception (Week 3-4)**
- [ ] Member CRUD with beautiful cards and tables
- [ ] Subscription plans with gold-tier badges
- [ ] Receptionist check-in/out with QR scan simulation
- [ ] Payment collection with branded receipts
- [ ] **Kiosk mode for self check-in**
- [ ] WhatsApp integration for auto-messages

### **Phase 3: Trainer + Member Portals (Week 5-6)**
- [ ] Trainer dashboard with member assignment
- [ ] Workout plan builder (drag-drop exercises)
- [ ] Member portal with digital card
- [ ] Progress tracking with charts
- [ ] **Progress photo upload with before/after slider**

### **Phase 4: Classes + Gamification (Week 7-8)**
- [ ] Group class scheduling and booking
- [ ] **XP system, badges, leaderboards**
- [ ] Achievement unlock animations
- [ ] Challenges creation and participation
- [ ] Trainer rating system

### **Phase 5: Advanced Features (Week 9-10)**
- [ ] Import/Export engine (streaming, 50k+ rows)
- [ ] Inventory/POS for supplements
- [ ] **In-app messaging**
- [ ] Advanced analytics with predictive churn
- [ ] Multi-language (English/Hindi/Gujarati)

### **Phase 6: Polish & Launch (Week 11)**
- [ ] PWA configuration
- [ ] Push notifications
- [ ] Performance audit (Lighthouse 95+)
- [ ] Mobile responsiveness testing
- [ ] **Deploy + Demo to the receptionist** 😉

---

## 🎁 BONUS: "IMPRESS HER" FEATURES

1. **🌅 Sunrise Animation** — Since the gym is in Sunrise Complex, the login page has a subtle golden sunrise animation behind the Eagle Gym logo.

2. **💎 Member Tiers Visual** — Bronze/Silver/Gold/Platinum/Diamond cards that look like actual premium credit cards with member photo and holographic effect.

3. **🎂 Birthday Surprise** — On member's birthday, the dashboard shows confetti + "Happy Birthday [Name]! Your protein shake is on us today!" Auto-notifies receptionist.

4. **📱 Shareable Progress** — Members can generate beautiful Instagram-story-style progress cards to share on social media (free marketing for the gym).

5. **🏆 "Member of the Month"** — Auto-calculated based on attendance + consistency. Featured on digital display at reception + member portal.

6. **🎙️ Voice Commands** — "Hey Eagle, show me today's revenue" (experimental, but impressive demo).

7. **🌙 Late Night Mode** — For 24/7 gyms, red-tinted UI for night shifts to reduce eye strain.

```tsx
// The Golden Stat Card
<StatCard

  value={1247}
  trend="+12%"
  trendUp
  sparklineData={[45,52,49,60,72,68,85]}
  glowColor="gold"
/>

// green trend badge with arrow.
```

```bash
npx tailwindcss init -p
```

### Step 2: Initialize shadcn/ui
```bash
npx shadcn-ui@latest init
```
When it asks:
- **Style**: Pick `New York` (cleaner, more modern)
- **Base color**: Pick `Neutral` or `Stone` (we'll override with our gold theme)
- **CSS variables**: Say **Yes**

### Step 3: Initialize Prisma
```bash
npx prisma init
```

This creates:
- `prisma/schema.prisma`
- `.env` file

### Step 4: Add your database URL to `.env`
```env
DATABASE_URL="postgresql://USER:PASSWORD@localhost:5432/eagle_gym?schema=public"
NEXTAUTH_SECRET="your-super-secret-key-here"
NEXTAUTH_URL="http://localhost:3000"
```

### Step 5: Create the schema
Write your `prisma/schema.prisma` with all the tables we discussed.

Kimi: **Stick with `pnpm + Node.js` for now.** Here's why:

---

## ⚡ The Honest Comparison

| | **pnpm + Node.js** (Current) | **Bun** |
|---|---|---|
| **Install Speed** | Fast (already done) | ⚡ 2-3x faster |
| **Runtime Speed** | Standard | ⚡ Faster for some ops |
| **Windows Support** | ✅ Rock solid | 🟡 Works, but less mature |
| **Next.js 14** | ✅ Officially supported | 🟡 Mostly works, edge cases |
| **Prisma** | ✅ First-class support | 🟡 Had issues historically |
| **Your Current State** | ✅ Everything installed & working | ❌ Would need full reinstall |
| **Risk of Weird Bugs** | Low | Higher on Windows |

---

## 🎯 My Recommendation

**Don't switch right now.** You're on **Windows**, you have **Next.js 14**, and you have **Prisma** — this is the exact combo where Bun can throw random errors that waste hours to debug.

> **Bun shines on Linux/macOS.** On Windows, it's still catching up.

### What to do instead:

1. **Keep pnpm for development** — it's already installed, fast, and reliable
2. **Use Node.js v22** — you already have it, it's LTS, perfect for Next.js 14
3. **Consider Bun later** — once your app is built and you're deploying to a **Linux server**, you can run it with Bun runtime for extra speed

---

## 🏆 The Real "Best Choice" for YOU

Since your goal is to **build fast and impress her**, the best choice is **whatever doesn't break**.

```
✅ pnpm + Node.js 22 + Next.js 14 = Battle-tested, works now, zero risk
⚠️  Bun + Windows + Prisma = Potential time sink, possible compatibility issues
```

**You've already won the setup battle.** Don't restart it.

---

## 💡 If You Still Want Bun Later

After the project is complete and deployed:
```bash
# On your Linux server:
bun run build
bun run start
```

Bun as a **production runtime** on Linux = excellent idea.  
Bun as a **development toolchain** on Windows with Prisma = unnecessary risk.

**Keep coding with what you have.** 🦅

**Next file:** `src/lib/utils.ts` (the `cn()` utility + general helpers)

Say **"next"** when ready. 🦅
User: next
Kimi: **File 3:** `src/lib/utils.ts`

```typescript
import { type ClassValue, clsx } from "clsx";
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge";
import { format, formatDistanceToNow } from "date-fns";

/**
 * Merge Tailwind classes with conflict resolution
 */
export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs));
}

/**
 * Format date to Indian standard
 */
export function formatDate(
  date: Date | string | number,
  pattern: string = "dd MMM yyyy"
): string {
  if (!date) return "-";
  const d = typeof date === "string" || typeof date === "number" ? new Date(date) : date;
  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return "-";
  return format(d, pattern);
}

/**
 * Format date to relative time (e.g., "2 hours ago")
 */
export function formatRelative(date: Date | string | number): string {
  if (!date) return "-";
  const d = typeof date === "string" || typeof date === "number" ? new Date(date) : date;
  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return "-";
  return formatDistanceToNow(d, { addSuffix: true });
}

/**
 * Format number to Indian currency (₹)
 */
export function formatCurrency(
  amount: number | string | null | undefined,
  options: { showSymbol?: boolean; decimals?: number } = {}
): string {
  const { showSymbol = true, decimals = 2 } = options;
  
  if (amount === null || amount === undefined || amount === "") return showSymbol ? "₹0.00" : "0.00";
  
  const num = typeof amount === "string" ? parseFloat(amount) : amount;
  if (isNaN(num)) return showSymbol ? "₹0.00" : "0.00";

  const formatter = new Intl.NumberFormat("en-IN", {
    style: "currency",
    currency: "INR",
    minimumFractionDigits: decimals,
    maximumFractionDigits: decimals,
  });

  const formatted = formatter.format(Math.abs(num));
  return num < 0 ? `-${formatted}` : formatted;
}

/**
 * Format number with Indian separators (1,24,500)
 */
export function formatNumber(
  num: number | string | null | undefined,
  decimals: number = 0
): string {
  if (num === null || num === undefined || num === "") return "0";
  
  const number = typeof num === "string" ? parseFloat(num) : num;
  if (isNaN(number)) return "0";

  return new Intl.NumberFormat("en-IN", {
    minimumFractionDigits: decimals,
    maximumFractionDigits: decimals,
  }).format(number);
}

/**
 * Truncate text with ellipsis
 */
export function truncate(str: string, length: number = 50): string {
  if (!str) return "";
  if (str.length <= length) return str;
  return str.slice(0, length).trim() + "...";
}

/**
 * Generate a random ID
 */
export function generateId(prefix: string = ""): string {
  const timestamp = Date.now().toString(36);
  const random = Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 8);
  return prefix ? `${prefix}_${timestamp}${random}` : `${timestamp}${random}`;
}

/**
 * Capitalize first letter of each word
 */
export function capitalize(str: string): string {
  if (!str) return "";
  return str
    .split(" ")
    .map((word) => word.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + word.slice(1).toLowerCase())
    .join(" ");
}

/**
 * Delay promise (for loaders, animations)
 */
export function delay(ms: number): Promise<void> {
  return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
}

/**
 * Debounce function
 */
export function debounce<T extends (...args: unknown[]) => unknown>(
  func: T,
  wait: number
): (...args: Parameters<T>) => void {
  let timeout: NodeJS.Timeout;
  return (...args: Parameters<T>) => {
    clearTimeout(timeout);
    timeout = setTimeout(() => func(...args), wait);
  };
}

/**
 * Deep clone an object
 */
export function deepClone<T>(obj: T): T {
  return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(obj));
}

/**
 * Check if value is empty (null, undefined, "", [], {})
 */
export function isEmpty(value: unknown): boolean {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) return true;
  if (typeof value === "string") return value.trim() === "";
  if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.length === 0;
  if (typeof value === "object") return Object.keys(value).length === 0;
  return false;
}

/**
 * Get initials from name (e.g., "Rahul Patel" -> "RP")
 */
export function getInitials(name: string): string {
  if (!name) return "??";
  return name
    .split(" ")
    .map((n) => n[0])
    .join("")
    .toUpperCase()
    .slice(0, 2);
}

/**
 * Get avatar color based on name (consistent colors)
 */
export function getAvatarColor(name: string): string {
  const colors = [
    "bg-gold-500/20 text-gold-400",
    "bg-electric-cyan/20 text-electric-cyan",
    "bg-neon-green/20 text-neon-green",
    "bg-crimson/20 text-crimson",
    "bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-400",
    "bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400",
  ];
  
  let hash = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < name.length; i++) {
    hash = name.charCodeAt(i) + ((hash << 5) - hash);
  }
  
  return colors[Math.abs(hash) % colors.length];
}

/**
 * Calculate percentage
 */
export function calculatePercentage(value: number, total: number): number {
  if (total === 0) return 0;
  return Math.round((value / total) * 100);
}

/**
 * File size formatter
 */
export function formatFileSize(bytes: number): string {
  if (bytes === 0) return "0 Bytes";
  const k = 1024;
  const sizes = ["Bytes", "KB", "MB", "GB"];
  const i = Math.floor(Math.log(bytes) / Math.log(k));
  return parseFloat((bytes / Math.pow(k, i)).toFixed(2)) + " " + sizes[i];
}

/**
 * Generate a random OTP
 */
export function generateOTP(length: number = 6): string {
  return Array.from({ length }, () => Math.floor(Math.random() * 10)).join("");
}

/**
 * Mask phone number (e.g., +91 98xxx xxxxx)
 */
export function maskPhone(phone: string): string {
  if (!phone || phone.length < 4) return phone;
  const visible = phone.slice(-4);
  const masked = phone.slice(0, -4).replace(/\d/g, "x");
  return masked + visible;
}

/**
 * Mask email (e.g., r****@gmail.com)
 */
export function maskEmail(email: string): string {
  if (!email || !email.includes("@")) return email;
  const [local, domain] = email.split("@");
  const maskedLocal = local[0] + "*".repeat(local.length - 1);
  return `${maskedLocal}@${domain}`;
}

/**
 * Check if device is mobile
 */
export function isMobile(): boolean {
  if (typeof window === "undefined") return false;
  return /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(
    navigator.userAgent
  );
}

/**
 * Scroll to element smoothly
 */
export function scrollToElement(elementId: string): void {
  const element = document.getElementById(elementId);
  if (element) {
    element.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "start" });
  }
}

/**
 * Copy to clipboard
 */
export async function copyToClipboard(text: string): Promise<boolean> {
  try {
    await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    return true;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

/**
 * Parse CSV safely
 */
export function parseCSV(text: string): string[][] {
  const lines = text.trim().split("\n");
  return lines.map((line) => {
    const result: string[] = [];
    let current = "";
    let inQuotes = false;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < line.length; i++) {
      const char = line[i];
      if (char === '"') {
        inQuotes = !inQuotes;
      } else if (char === "," && !inQuotes) {
        result.push(current.trim());
        current = "";
      } else {
        current += char;
      }
    }
    result.push(current.trim());
    return result;
  });
}

/**
 * Slugify text (for URLs)
 */
export function slugify(text: string): string {
  return text
    .toString()
    .toLowerCase()
    .trim()
    .replace(/\s+/g, "-")
    .replace(/[^\w\-]+/g, "")
    .replace(/\-\-+/g, "-");
}

/**
 * Get greeting based on time
 */
export function getGreeting(): string {
  const hour = new Date().getHours();
  if (hour < 12) return "Good Morning";
  if (hour < 17) return "Good Afternoon";
  if (hour < 21) return "Good Evening";
  return "Good Night";
}
```

```typescript
import { z } from "zod";
import { GENDER, BLOOD_GROUP, PAYMENT_METHOD, CLASS_CATEGORIES, EQUIPMENT_CATEGORIES } from "./constants";

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// COMMON / SHARED SCHEMAS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

export const PaginationSchema = z.object({
  page: z.coerce.number().min(1).default(1),
  limit: z.coerce.number().min(1).max(100).default(10),
  search: z.string().optional(),
  sortBy: z.string().optional(),
  sortOrder: z.enum(["asc", "desc"]).optional().default("desc"),
});

export const DateRangeSchema = z.object({
  from: z.string().datetime().optional(),
  to: z.string().datetime().optional(),
});

export const IdSchema = z.object({
  id: z.string().cuid({ message: "Invalid ID format" }),
});

export const EmailSchema = z
  .string()
  .min(1, "Email is required")
  .email("Please enter a valid email address");

export const PhoneSchema = z
  .string()
  .min(1, "Phone number is required")
  .regex(/^[6-9]\d{9}$/, "Please enter a valid 10-digit Indian mobile number");

export const PasswordSchema = z
  .string()
  .min(8, "Password must be at least 8 characters")
  .max(100, "Password is too long")
  .regex(/[A-Z]/, "Password must contain at least one uppercase letter")
  .regex(/[a-z]/, "Password must contain at least one lowercase letter")
  .regex(/[0-9]/, "Password must contain at least one number")
  .regex(/[^A-Za-z0-9]/, "Password must contain at least one special character");

export const NameSchema = z
  .string()
  .min(2, "Name must be at least 2 characters")
  .max(50, "Name must be less than 50 characters")
  .regex(/^[a-zA-Z\s]+$/, "Name can only contain letters and spaces");

export const AddressSchema = z.object({
  street: z.string().min(1, "Street is required").max(200),
  city: z.string().min(1, "City is required").max(50),
  state: z.string().min(1, "State is required").max(50),
  pincode: z
    .string()
    .regex(/^\d{6}$/, "Please enter a valid 6-digit PIN code"),
  country: z.string().default("India"),
});

export const FileUploadSchema = z.object({
  file: z
    .instanceof(File)
    .refine((file) => file.size <= 5 * 1024 * 1024, "File size must be less than 5MB")
    .refine(
      (file) => ["image/jpeg", "image/png", "image/webp", "image/jpg"].includes(file.type),
      "Only JPG, PNG, and WebP images are allowed"
    ),
});

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// AUTH SCHEMAS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

export const LoginSchema = z.object({
  email: EmailSchema,
  password: z.string().min(1, "Password is required"),
  rememberMe: z.boolean().optional().default(false),
});

export const RegisterSchema = z
  .object({
    firstName: NameSchema,
    lastName: NameSchema,
    email: EmailSchema,
    phone: PhoneSchema,
    password: PasswordSchema,
    confirmPassword: z.string().min(1, "Please confirm your password"),
    gender: z.enum(["MALE", "FEMALE", "OTHER", "PREFER_NOT_TO_SAY"]).optional(),
    dateOfBirth: z
      .string()
      .optional()
      .refine((val) => {
        if (!val) return true;
        const date = new Date(val);
        const now = new Date();
        const age = now.getFullYear() - date.getFullYear();
        return age >= 12 && age <= 100;
      }, "Age must be between 12 and 100 years"),
    termsAccepted: z.literal(true, {
      errorMap: () => ({ message: "You must accept the terms and conditions" }),
    }),
  })
  .refine((data) => data.password === data.confirmPassword, {
    message: "Passwords do not match",
    path: ["confirmPassword"],
  });

export const ForgotPasswordSchema = z.object({
  email: EmailSchema,
});

export const ResetPasswordSchema = z
  .object({
    token: z.string().min(1, "Invalid reset token"),
    password: PasswordSchema,
    confirmPassword: z.string().min(1, "Please confirm your password"),
  })
  .refine((data) => data.password === data.confirmPassword, {
    message: "Passwords do not match",
    path: ["confirmPassword"],
  });

export const OTPSchema = z.object({
  otp: z
    .string()
    .length(6, "OTP must be 6 digits")
    .regex(/^\d{6}$/, "OTP must contain only numbers"),
});

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// USER SCHEMAS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

export const CreateUserSchema = z.object({
  firstName: NameSchema,
  lastName: NameSchema,
  email: EmailSchema,
  phone: PhoneSchema,
  password: PasswordSchema.optional(),
  role: z.enum(["SUPER_ADMIN", "ADMIN", "RECEPTIONIST", "TRAINER", "MEMBER", "WORKER"]),
  status: z.enum(["ACTIVE", "INACTIVE", "SUSPENDED", "PENDING"]).default("ACTIVE"),
  avatar: z.string().url().optional().or(z.literal("")),
});

export const UpdateUserSchema = z.object({
  firstName: NameSchema.optional(),
  lastName: NameSchema.optional(),
  email: EmailSchema.optional(),
  phone: PhoneSchema.optional(),
  avatar: z.string().url().optional().or(z.literal("")),
  status: z.enum(["ACTIVE", "INACTIVE", "SUSPENDED", "PENDING"]).optional(),
});

export const UpdateProfileSchema = z.object({
  firstName: NameSchema,
  lastName: NameSchema,
  phone: PhoneSchema,
  avatar: z.string().optional(),
});

export const ChangePasswordSchema = z
  .object({
    currentPassword: z.string().min(1, "Current password is required"),
    newPassword: PasswordSchema,
    confirmPassword: z.string().min(1, "Please confirm your password"),
  })
  .refine((data) => data.newPassword === data.confirmPassword, {
    message: "Passwords do not match",
    path: ["confirmPassword"],
  });

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MEMBER SCHEMAS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

export const CreateMemberSchema = z.object({
  firstName: NameSchema,
  lastName: NameSchema,
  email: EmailSchema,
  phone: PhoneSchema,
  gender: z.enum(["MALE", "FEMALE", "OTHER", "PREFER_NOT_TO_SAY"]).optional(),
  dateOfBirth: z.string().optional(),
  bloodGroup: z.enum(["A+", "A-", "B+", "B-", "AB+", "AB-", "O+", "O-"]).optional(),
  emergencyContact: z
    .string()
    .regex(/^[6-9]\d{9}$/, "Please enter a valid 10-digit number")
    .optional()
    .or(z.literal("")),
  address: z.string().max(500).optional(),
  city: z.string().max(50).optional(),
  state: z.string().max(50).optional(),
  pincode: z.string().regex(/^\d{6}$/).optional().or(z.literal("")),
  planId: z.string().cuid({ message: "Please select a subscription plan" }),
  startDate: z.string().min(1, "Start date is required"),
  amount: z.coerce.number().min(0, "Amount must be positive"),
  paymentMethod: z.enum(["CASH", "CARD", "UPI", "ONLINE", "CHEQUE", "BANK_TRANSFER", "EMI"]),
  trainerId: z.string().cuid().optional().or(z.literal("")),
  source: z.string().optional(), // How they heard about the gym
  notes: z.string().max(1000).optional(),
});

export const UpdateMemberSchema = z.object({
  firstName: NameSchema.optional(),
  lastName: NameSchema.optional(),
  email: EmailSchema.optional(),
  phone: PhoneSchema.optional(),
  gender: z.enum(["MALE", "FEMALE", "OTHER", "PREFER_NOT_TO_SAY"]).optional(),
  dateOfBirth: z.string().optional(),
  bloodGroup: z.enum(["A+", "A-", "B+", "B-", "AB+", "AB-", "O+", "O-"]).optional(),
  emergencyContact: z
    .string()
    .regex(/^[6-9]\d{9}$/)
    .optional()
    .or(z.literal("")),
  address: z.string().max(500).optional(),
  city: z.string().max(50).optional(),
  state: z.string().max(50).optional(),
  pincode: z.string().regex(/^\d{6}$/).optional().or(z.literal("")),
  trainerId: z.string().cuid().optional().or(z.literal("")),
  status: z.enum(["ACTIVE", "INACTIVE", "EXPIRED", "FROZEN", "PENDING"]).optional(),
  notes: z.string().max(1000).optional(),
});

export const MemberFilterSchema = PaginationSchema.merge(
  z.object({
    status: z.enum(["ACTIVE", "INACTIVE", "EXPIRED", "FROZEN", "PENDING", "ALL"]).optional(),
    planId: z.string().optional(),
    trainerId: z.string().optional(),
    gender: z.enum(["MALE", "FEMALE", "OTHER", "PREFER_NOT_TO_SAY", "ALL"]).optional(),
    dateRange: DateRangeSchema.optional(),
    hasDue: z.boolean().optional(),
  })
);

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// TRAINER SCHEMAS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

export const CreateTrainerSchema = z.object({
  firstName: NameSchema,
  lastName: NameSchema,
  email: EmailSchema,
  phone: PhoneSchema,
  password: PasswordSchema.optional(),
  specialization: z.array(z.string()).min(1, "Select at least one specialization"),
  experience: z.coerce.number().min(0, "Experience cannot be negative").max(50, "Too much experience"),
  salary: z.coerce.number().min(0).optional(),
  certifications: z.array(z.string()).optional(),
  bio: z.string().max(1000).optional(),
  availableDays: z.array(z.enum(["MON", "TUE", "WED", "THU", "FRI", "SAT", "SUN"])).min(1),
  availableFrom: z.string().regex(/^([01]\d|2[0-3]):([0-5]\d)$/, "Invalid time format (HH:MM)"),
  availableTo: z.string().regex(/^([01]\d|2[0-3]):([0-5]\d)$/, "Invalid time format (HH:MM)"),
});

export const UpdateTrainerSchema = CreateTrainerSchema.partial().omit({ password: true });

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// RECEPTIONIST / STAFF SCHEMAS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

export const CreateStaffSchema = z.object({
  firstName: NameSchema,
  lastName: NameSchema,
  email: EmailSchema,
  phone: PhoneSchema,
  password: PasswordSchema.optional(),
  role: z.enum(["RECEPTIONIST", "WORKER"]),
  shiftStart: z.string().regex(/^([01]\d|2[0-3]):([0-5]\d)$/, "Invalid time format"),
  shiftEnd: z.string().regex(/^([01]\d|2[0-3]):([0-5]\d)$/, "Invalid time format"),
  salary: z.coerce.number().min(0).optional(),
  joiningDate: z.string().optional(),
});

export const UpdateStaffSchema = CreateStaffSchema.partial().omit({ password: true });

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SUBSCRIPTION PLAN SCHEMAS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

export const CreatePlanSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(2, "Plan name is required").max(50),
  duration: z.coerce.number().min(1, "Duration must be at least 1 day").max(3650, "Duration too long"),
  price: z.coerce.number().min(0, "Price cannot be negative"),
  gstIncluded: z.boolean().default(true),
  features: z.array(z.string().min(1)).min(1, "Add at least one feature"),
  description: z.string().max(500).optional(),
  color: z.string().max(20).optional(),
  isActive: z.boolean().default(true),
  maxCheckIns: z.coerce.number().min(0).optional(), // 0 = unlimited
  ptSessions: z.coerce.number().min(0).optional(),
  guestPasses: z.coerce.number().min(0).optional(),
  sortOrder: z.coerce.number().default(0),
});

export const UpdatePlanSchema = CreatePlanSchema.partial();

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SUBSCRIPTION SCHEMAS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

  notes: z.string().optional(),
  autoRenew: z.boolean().default(false),
});

});

// PAYMENT SCHEMAS

export const CreatePaymentSchema = z.object({
  memberId: z.string().cuid(),
  amount: z.coerce.number().min(1, "Amount must be greater than 0"),
  method: z.enum(["CASH", "CARD", "UPI", "ONLINE", "CHEQUE", "BANK_TRANSFER", "EMI"]),
  type: z.enum(["SUBSCRIPTION", "PT_SESSION", "PRODUCT", "OTHER"]).default("SUBSCRIPTION"),
  subscriptionId: z.string().cuid().optional(),
  description: z.string().max(500).optional(),
  transactionId: z.string().optional(), // For online payments
  discount: z.coerce.number().min(0).default(0),
  tax: z.coerce.number().min(0).default(0),
});

export const PaymentFilterSchema = PaginationSchema.merge(
  z.object({
    memberId: z.string().optional(),
    method: z.enum(["CASH", "CARD", "UPI", "ONLINE", "CHEQUE", "BANK_TRANSFER", "EMI", "ALL"]).optional(),
    status: z.enum(["PENDING", "COMPLETED", "FAILED", "REFUNDED", "PARTIAL", "ALL"]).optional(),
    type: z.enum(["SUBSCRIPTION", "PT_SESSION", "PRODUCT", "OTHER", "ALL"]).optional(),
    dateRange: DateRangeSchema.optional(),
  })
);

});

    date: z.string().optional(),

);

export const CreateClassSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(2, "Class name is required").max(100),
  description: z.string().max(1000).optional(),
  category: z.enum(["YOGA", "ZUMBA", "CROSSFIT", "PILATES", "SPINNING", "HIIT", "BOXING", "DANCE", "MEDITATION", "AEROBICS"]),
  trainerId: z.string().cuid(),
  maxCapacity: z.coerce.number().min(1, "Capacity must be at least 1").max(100),
  duration: z.coerce.number().min(15, "Minimum 15 minutes").max(180, "Maximum 3 hours"),
  color: z.string().max(20).optional(),
  isActive: z.boolean().default(true),
});

export const CreateScheduleSchema = z.object({
  classId: z.string().cuid(),
  dayOfWeek: z.coerce.number().min(0).max(6),
  startTime: z.string().regex(/^([01]\d|2[0-3]):([0-5]\d)$/, "Invalid time format"),
  room: z.string().min(1, "Room name is required").max(50),
});

export const BookClassSchema = z.object({
  scheduleId: z.string().cuid(),
  memberId: z.string().cuid(),
});

  bookingId: z.string().cuid(),
  reason: z.string().max(500).optional(),
});

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// WORKOUT SCHEMAS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

export const ExerciseSchema = z.object({
  name: z.string().min(1, "Exercise name is required"),
  muscleGroup: z.string().optional(),
  sets: z.coerce.number().min(1).max(50).default(3),
  reps: z.coerce.number().min(1).max(100).default(10),
  weight: z.coerce.number().min(0).optional(),
  duration: z.coerce.number().min(0).optional(), // seconds
  rest: z.coerce.number().min(0).default(60), // seconds
  notes: z.string().max(500).optional(),
  videoUrl: z.string().url().optional().or(z.literal("")),
});
```

**Next file:** `src/lib/rbac.ts` (Role-based access control logic)

Say **"next"** when ready. 🦅
User: next
Kimi: **File 6:** `src/lib/rbac.ts`

```typescript
import { ROLES, ROLE_HIERARCHY, ROLE_PERMISSIONS, PERMISSIONS } from "./constants";
import type { Role, Permission } from "./constants";

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 🦅 EAGLE GYM — Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

/**
 * Check if a role has a specific permission
 */
export function hasPermission(role: Role, permission: Permission): boolean {
  if (!role || !permission) return false;
  const permissions = ROLE_PERMISSIONS[role];
  if (!permissions) return false;
  return permissions.includes(permission);
}

/**
 * Check if a role has ANY of the given permissions
 */
export function hasAnyPermission(role: Role, permissions: Permission[]): boolean {
  if (!role || !permissions.length) return false;
  return permissions.some((p) => hasPermission(role, p));
}

/**
 * Check if a role has ALL of the given permissions
 */
export function hasAllPermissions(role: Role, permissions: Permission[]): boolean {
  if (!role || !permissions.length) return false;
  return permissions.every((p) => hasPermission(role, p));
}

/**
 * Check if role A can manage role B (hierarchy check)
 * Super Admin can manage everyone
 * Admin can manage everyone except Super Admin and other Admins
 */
export function canManageRole(managerRole: Role, targetRole: Role): boolean {
  if (managerRole === ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN) return true;
  if (managerRole === ROLES.ADMIN) {
    return targetRole !== ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN && targetRole !== ROLES.ADMIN;
  }
  return false;
}

/**
 * Check if a user can access a specific resource (ownership check)
 * Users can always access their own resources
 * Higher roles can access lower role resources
 */
export function canAccessResource(
  userRole: Role,
  userId: string,
  resourceOwnerId: string,
  requiredPermission: Permission
): boolean {
  // Own resource
  if (userId === resourceOwnerId) return true;
  // Has explicit permission
  if (hasPermission(userRole, requiredPermission)) return true;
  return false;
}

/**
 * Check if role A has higher or equal hierarchy than role B
 */
export function isRoleHigherOrEqual(roleA: Role, roleB: Role): boolean {
  return (ROLE_HIERARCHY[roleA] ?? 0) >= (ROLE_HIERARCHY[roleB] ?? 0);
}

/**
 * Check if role A is strictly higher than role B
 */
export function isRoleHigher(roleA: Role, roleB: Role): boolean {
  return (ROLE_HIERARCHY[roleA] ?? 0) > (ROLE_HIERARCHY[roleB] ?? 0);
}

/**
 * Get all permissions for a role
 */
export function getRolePermissions(role: Role): Permission[] {
  return ROLE_PERMISSIONS[role] ?? [];
}

/**
 * Get permissions that Admin is RESTRICTED from (vs Super Admin)
 * These are the ~2-5% restrictions Super Admin can toggle
 */
export function getAdminRestrictedPermissions(): Permission[] {
  return [
    PERMISSIONS.ADMIN_CREATE,
    PERMISSIONS.ADMIN_READ,
    PERMISSIONS.ADMIN_UPDATE,
    PERMISSIONS.ADMIN_DELETE,
    PERMISSIONS.ADMIN_PERMISSIONS,
    PERMISSIONS.PLAN_DELETE,
    PERMISSIONS.SYSTEM_CONFIG,
    PERMISSIONS.AUDIT_READ,
    PERMISSIONS.EXPORT_UNLIMITED,
    PERMISSIONS.ANALYTICS_CHURN,
  ];
}

/**
 * Check if Admin has a specific restriction
 */
export function isAdminRestricted(permission: Permission): boolean {
  return getAdminRestrictedPermissions().includes(permission);
}

/**
 * Filter permissions — remove restricted ones for Admin
 * Super Admin passes all, Admin gets filtered
 */
export function filterPermissionsByRole(
  role: Role,
  permissions: Permission[]
): Permission[] {
  if (role === ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN) return permissions;
  if (role === ROLES.ADMIN) {
    const restricted = getAdminRestrictedPermissions();
    return permissions.filter((p) => !restricted.includes(p));
  }
  return permissions.filter((p) => hasPermission(role, p));
}

/**
 * Middleware helper: Check route access
 */
export function canAccessRoute(role: Role, routePrefix: string): boolean {
  const routeMap: Record<string, Role[]> = {
    "/super-admin": [ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN],
    "/admin": [ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN, ROLES.ADMIN],
    "/receptionist": [ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN, ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.RECEPTIONIST],
    "/trainer": [ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN, ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.TRAINER],
    "/member": [ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN, ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.RECEPTIONIST, ROLES.TRAINER, ROLES.MEMBER],
    "/worker": [ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN, ROLES.ADMIN, ROLES.WORKER],
  };

  for (const [prefix, allowedRoles] of Object.entries(routeMap)) {
    if (routePrefix.startsWith(prefix)) {
      return allowedRoles.includes(role);
    }
  }
  return false;
}

/**
 * Get dashboard home path based on role
 */
export function getRoleDashboard(role: Role): string {
  const dashboardMap: Record<Role, string> = {
    SUPER_ADMIN: "/super-admin",
    ADMIN: "/admin",
    RECEPTIONIST: "/receptionist",
    TRAINER: "/trainer",
    MEMBER: "/member",
    WORKER: "/worker",
  };
  return dashboardMap[role] ?? "/";
}

/**
 * Get readable role label
 */
export function getRoleLabel(role: Role): string {
  const labels: Record<Role, string> = {
    SUPER_ADMIN: "Super Admin",
    ADMIN: "Admin",
    RECEPTIONIST: "Receptionist",
    TRAINER: "Trainer",
    MEMBER: "Member",
    WORKER: "Staff",
  };
  return labels[role] ?? role;
}

/**
 * Get role badge color class
 */
export function getRoleBadgeClass(role: Role): string {
  const classes: Record<Role, string> = {
    SUPER_ADMIN: "bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-400 border-purple-500/30",
    ADMIN: "bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/30",
    RECEPTIONIST: "bg-electric-cyan/20 text-electric-cyan border-electric-cyan/30",
    TRAINER: "bg-neon-green/20 text-neon-green border-neon-green/30",
    MEMBER: "bg-gold-500/20 text-gold-400 border-gold-500/30",
    WORKER: "bg-obsidian-400/20 text-obsidian-300 border-obsidian-400/30",
  };
  return classes[role] ?? "bg-obsidian-500/20 text-obsidian-300";
}

/**
 * Permission guard component helper
 * Returns true/false for conditional rendering
 */
export function usePermission(role: Role | undefined | null, permission: Permission): boolean {
  if (!role) return false;
  return hasPermission(role, permission);
}

/**
 * Check if user can perform bulk operations
 */
export function canBulkOperate(role: Role): boolean {
  return hasAnyPermission(role, [
    PERMISSIONS.MEMBER_BULK,
    PERMISSIONS.IMPORT_DATA,
    PERMISSIONS.EXPORT_DATA,
  ]);
}

/**
 * Check export limit based on role
 */
export function getExportLimit(role: Role): number {
  if (role === ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN) return 100000;
  if (role === ROLES.ADMIN) return 5000;
  return 0;
}

/**
 * Validate that a role assignment is legal
 * (e.g., Admin cannot create Super Admin)
 */
export function isValidRoleAssignment(
  assignerRole: Role,
  targetRole: Role
): { valid: boolean; reason?: string } {
  if (assignerRole === ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN) return { valid: true };

  if (assignerRole === ROLES.ADMIN) {
    if (targetRole === ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN) {
      return { valid: false, reason: "Admin cannot assign Super Admin role" };
    }
    if (targetRole === ROLES.ADMIN) {
      return { valid: false, reason: "Admin cannot assign Admin role" };
    }
    return { valid: true };
  }

  return {
    valid: false,
    reason: "You don't have permission to assign roles",
  };
}

/**
 * Role-based sidebar navigation filter
 * Returns allowed nav items based on role
 */
export function getAllowedNavItems<T extends { requiredPermission?: Permission }>(
  role: Role,
  items: T[]
): T[] {
  return items.filter((item) => {
    if (!item.requiredPermission) return true;
    return hasPermission(role, item.requiredPermission);
  });
}
```

```typescript
import { PrismaClient } from "@prisma/client";

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 🦅 EAGLE GYM — Prisma Client Singleton
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

const globalForPrisma = globalThis as unknown as {
  prisma: PrismaClient | undefined;
};

export const prisma =
  globalForPrisma.prisma ??
  new PrismaClient({
    log:
      process.env.NODE_ENV === "development"
        ? ["query", "error", "warn"]
        : ["error"],
  });

if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production") globalForPrisma.prisma = prisma;

export default prisma;
```

```prisma
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// 🦅 EAGLE GYM — Prisma Database Schema
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

generator client {
  provider = "prisma-client-js"
}

datasource db {
  provider = "postgresql"
  url      = env("DATABASE_URL")
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ENUMS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

enum Role {
  SUPER_ADMIN
  ADMIN
  RECEPTIONIST
  TRAINER
  MEMBER
  WORKER
}

enum UserStatus {
  ACTIVE
  INACTIVE
  SUSPENDED
  PENDING
}

enum MemberStatus {
  ACTIVE
  INACTIVE
  EXPIRED
  FROZEN
  PENDING
}

enum Gender {
  MALE
  FEMALE
  OTHER
  PREFER_NOT_TO_SAY
}

enum SubscriptionStatus {
  ACTIVE
  EXPIRED
  CANCELLED
  FROZEN
  PENDING
  GRACE
}

enum PaymentStatus {
  PENDING
  COMPLETED
  FAILED
  REFUNDED
  PARTIAL
}

enum PaymentMethod {

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// CORE USER
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

model User {
  id            String     @id @default(cuid())
  email         String     @unique
  phone         String?    @unique
  password      String
  firstName     String
  lastName      String
  avatar        String?
  role          Role       @default(MEMBER)
  status        UserStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  emailVerified DateTime?
  phoneVerified DateTime?
  lastLoginAt   DateTime?
  lastLoginIp   String?
  createdAt     DateTime   @default(now())
  updatedAt     DateTime   @updatedAt

  // Relations
  member        Member?
  trainer       Trainer?
  receptionist  Receptionist?
  admin         Admin?
  superAdmin    SuperAdmin?
  worker        Worker?
  sessions      Session[]
  notifications Notification[]
  auditLogs     AuditLog[]
  sentMessages  Message[] @relation("SentMessages")
  receivedMessages Message[] @relation("ReceivedMessages")
  achievements  UserAchievement[]
  xpTransactions XPTransaction[]

  @@index([email])
  @@index([phone])
  @@index([role])
  @@index([status])
  @@map("users")
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SESSION (NextAuth)
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

model Session {
  id           String   @id @default(cuid())
  sessionToken String   @unique
  userId       String
  expires      DateTime
  user         User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@index([userId])
  @@map("sessions")
}

model VerificationToken {
  identifier String
  token      String   @unique
  expires    DateTime

  @@unique([identifier, token])
  @@map("verification_tokens")
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MEMBER
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

model Member {
  id                String   @id @default(cuid())
  userId            String   @unique
  user              User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  // Physical
  dateOfBirth       DateTime?
  gender            Gender?
  bloodGroup        String?
  emergencyContact  String?
  address           String?
  city              String?
  state             String?
  pincode           String?
  country           String   @default("India")

  // Gym Specific
  joinDate          DateTime @default(now())
  source            String?  // How they heard about gym
  notes             String?  @db.Text
  status            MemberStatus @default(ACTIVE)

  // Relations
  subscription      Subscription?
  attendance        Attendance[]
  progress          Progress[]
  progressPhotos    ProgressPhoto[]
  workouts          WorkoutLog[]
  dietPlans         DietPlan[] @relation("MemberDietPlans")
  payments          Payment[]
  classBookings     ClassBooking[]
  goals             Goal[]
  trainerId         String?
  trainer           Trainer? @relation(fields: [trainerId], references: [id])
  messages          Message[]
  documents         Document[]
  notifications     Notification[]

  @@index([status])
  @@index([trainerId])
  @@index([joinDate])
  @@map("members")
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// TRAINER
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

model Trainer {
  id             String   @id @default(cuid())
  userId         String   @unique
  user           User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  specialization String[]
  experience     Int      @default(0)
  salary         Decimal? @db.Decimal(10, 2)
  bio            String?  @db.Text
  certifications String[]
  rating         Float    @default(0)
  totalRatings   Int      @default(0)
  isActive       Boolean  @default(true)

  // Availability
  availableDays  String[] // ["MON","TUE","WED"]
  availableFrom  String   @default("06:00") // HH:MM
  availableTo    String   @default("22:00") // HH:MM

  createdAt      DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt      DateTime @updatedAt

  // Relations
  members        Member[]
  classes        GymClass[]
  schedules      Schedule[]
  sessions       PTSession[]
  workouts       WorkoutPlan[]
  dietPlans      DietPlan[] @relation("TrainerDietPlans")
  messages       Message[]

  @@index([isActive])
  @@map("trainers")
}

  shiftStart  String   @default("06:00")
  shiftEnd    String   @default("22:00")
  salary      Decimal? @db.Decimal(10, 2)
  joiningDate DateTime @default(now())
  isActive    Boolean  @default(true)

  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt

  @@map("receptionists")
}

  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

model Worker {

  userId      String   @unique
  user        User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  department  String   @default("GENERAL") // CLEANING, MAINTENANCE, SECURITY
  shiftStart  String   @default("06:00")
  shiftEnd    String   @default("22:00")

  joiningDate DateTime @default(now())
  isActive    Boolean  @default(true)

  // Relations

  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt

  @@map("workers")
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SUBSCRIPTION PLANS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

model Plan {
  id            String   @id @default(cuid())
  name          String
  duration      Int      // days
  price         Decimal  @db.Decimal(10, 2)
  gstIncluded   Boolean  @default(true)
  features      String[]
  description   String?  @db.Text
  color         String?
  isActive      Boolean  @default(true)
  maxCheckIns   Int      @default(0) // 0 = unlimited
  ptSessions    Int      @default(0)
  guestPasses   Int      @default(0)
  sortOrder     Int      @default(0)

  createdBy     String
  createdAt     DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt     DateTime @updatedAt

  // Relations
  subscriptions Subscription[]

  @@index([isActive])
  @@index([sortOrder])
  @@map("plans")
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SUBSCRIPTION
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

model Subscription {
  id          String             @id @default(cuid())
  memberId    String             @unique
  member      Member             @relation(fields: [memberId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  planId      String
  plan        Plan               @relation(fields: [planId], references: [id])

  startDate   DateTime
  endDate     DateTime
  amount      Decimal            @db.Decimal(10, 2)
  discount    Decimal            @default(0) @db.Decimal(10, 2)
  status      SubscriptionStatus @default(ACTIVE)
  autoRenew   Boolean            @default(false)
  freezeUntil DateTime?

  createdAt   DateTime           @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime           @updatedAt

  @@index([status])
  @@index([endDate])
  @@index([memberId])
  @@map("subscriptions")
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PAYMENTS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

model Payment {
  id            String        @id @default(cuid())
  memberId      String
  member        Member        @relation(fields: [memberId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  amount        Decimal       @db.Decimal(10, 2)
  tax           Decimal       @default(0) @db.Decimal(10, 2)
  discount      Decimal       @default(0) @db.Decimal(10, 2)
  total         Decimal       @db.Decimal(10, 2)
  method        PaymentMethod
  type          PaymentType   @default(SUBSCRIPTION)
  status        PaymentStatus @default(PENDING)
  receiptNo     String        @unique
  transactionId String?
  description   String?

  subscriptionId String?
  saleId         String?

  createdAt     DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt     DateTime      @updatedAt

  @@index([memberId])
  @@index([status])
  @@index([createdAt])
  @@index([receiptNo])
  @@map("payments")
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ATTENDANCE

model Attendance {
  id        String           @id @default(cuid())

  date      DateTime         @default(now()) @db.Date
  checkIn   DateTime
  checkOut  DateTime?

  mode      AttendanceMode   @default(MANUAL)
  deviceInfo String?

  createdAt DateTime         @default(now())

  @@unique([memberId, date])
  @@index([memberId])
  @@index([date])
  @@index([status])
  @@map("attendance")
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// GROUP CLASSES
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

model GymClass {
  id          String        @id @default(cuid())
  name        String
  description String?       @db.Text
  category    ClassCategory
  trainerId   String
  trainer     Trainer       @relation(fields: [trainerId], references: [id])

  maxCapacity Int
  duration    Int           // minutes
  color       String?
  isActive    Boolean       @default(true)

  createdAt   DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime      @updatedAt

  // Relations
  schedules   ClassSchedule[]

  @@index([category])
  @@index([isActive])
  @@map("gym_classes")
}

model ClassSchedule {
  id        String   @id @default(cuid())
  classId   String
  class     GymClass @relation(fields: [classId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  dayOfWeek Int      // 0-6
  startTime String   // HH:MM
  room      String

  createdAt DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt DateTime @updatedAt

  // Relations
  bookings  ClassBooking[]

  @@index([classId])
  @@index([dayOfWeek])
  @@map("class_schedules")
}

model ClassBooking {
  id         String        @id @default(cuid())
  scheduleId String
  schedule   ClassSchedule @relation(fields: [scheduleId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  memberId   String
  member     Member        @relation(fields: [memberId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  status     BookingStatus @default(CONFIRMED)
  bookedAt   DateTime      @default(now())
  cancelledAt DateTime?
  cancelReason String?

  @@unique([scheduleId, memberId])
  @@index([memberId])
  @@index([status])
  @@map("class_bookings")
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

  memberId    String
```
